	function popWebPlayerNotification() {
		var flag = Cookies.get("wpn");
		if(!flag)
			$(".slogan .tip").show();
		else
			$(".slogan .tip").hide();
	};
	
	function closeWebPlayerNotification() {
		Cookies.set("wpn", "Y", {expires:365*50, path:"/", domain:document.domain});
		$(".slogan .tip").hide();
	}
	
	function headerCommonBannerLoad(url){
// 		url = window.location.href; //테스트용
		
		if(url.indexOf("?") > 0){
			url = url.substring(0,url.indexOf("?"))
		}

		if(url == g_urlWww || url == g_urlWww+"/" || url == g_urlWww+"/index" || url == g_urlMusic){ //main
			if(typeof window._headerCommonBannerSubList != "undefined" && window._headerCommonBannerMainList.length > 0){
				var selectedBanner = bugs.utils.getBannerRandomExtractByWeight(window._headerCommonBannerMainList);
				$('#header div.header div.banner').empty();
				$('#header div.header div.banner').append('<a href="'+ bugs.common_util.setLinkUrlWiseLog(selectedBanner.link, "M_header_03_03") +'" target="'+selectedBanner.target+'" onclick="bugs.logging.banner('+selectedBanner.banner_id+','+"'banner'"+')" title="'+selectedBanner.title+'-페이지 이동">'+
						'<img src="'+selectedBanner.image_path+'" alt="'+selectedBanner.title+'"></a>');
			}
		
		}else{ //sub
			if(typeof window._headerCommonBannerSubList != "undefined" && window._headerCommonBannerSubList.length > 0){
				var selectedBanner = bugs.utils.getBannerRandomExtractByWeight(window._headerCommonBannerSubList);
				$('#header div.header div.banner').empty();
				$('#header div.header div.banner').append('<a href="'+selectedBanner.link+'" target="'+selectedBanner.target+'" onclick="bugs.logging.banner('+selectedBanner.banner_id+','+"'banner'"+')" title="'+selectedBanner.title+'-페이지 이동">'+
						'<img src="'+selectedBanner.image_path+'" alt="'+selectedBanner.title+'"></a>');
			}
		}

	};

<script type="text/javascript">
//	var ua = navigator.userAgent;
//	window._isMacBrowser = navigator.userAgent.search("Mac") > -1;
//	window._isMacPlayerLinked = /Mac OS X 11_/.test(ua)
//				|| /Mac OS X 12_/.test(ua)
//				|| (/Mac OS X 10_/.test(ua) && !/Mac OS X 10_10/.test(ua) && !/Mac OS X 10_9/.test(ua) && !/Mac OS X 10_8/.test(ua) && !/Mac OS X 10_7/.test(ua) && !/Mac OS X 10_6/.test(ua) && !/Mac OS X 10_5/.test(ua)
//														&& !/Mac OS X 10_4/.test(ua) && !/Mac OS X 10_3/.test(ua) && !/Mac OS X 10_2/.test(ua));

	var goServiceGuidePlayerPage = function(){
		if(navigator.platform.indexOf('Win') > -1){
			document.location.href = "https://music.bugs.co.kr/serviceGuide/pc/bugsPlayer";
		}else{
			document.location.href = "https://music.bugs.co.kr/serviceGuide/pc/bugsPlayer?sub=macPlayer";
		}
	}

	$(document).ready(function() {
		showMacPlayerSelection();
	});

	var showMacPlayerSelection = function() {
		if(bugs.music.isMacPlayerSupport()) {
			$(".slogan .selectPlayer").show();
			$(".slogan .bugsPlayer").hide();

			var dp = bugs.cookie.get('defaultPlayer') || "";

			updateHeaderPlayerMenu(dp);
		} else {
			$(".slogan .selectPlayer").hide();
			$(".slogan .bugsPlayer").show();
		}
	}

	var updateHeaderPlayerMenu = function(type) {
		$("#headerWebPlayer").hide();
		$("#headerMacPlayer").hide();

		if(type == "MAC") {
			$("#headerMacPlayer").show();
		} else { // if(type == "" || type == "WEB") {
			$("#headerWebPlayer").show();
			$("#headerWebPlayer").removeAttr("onclick");
			$("#headerWebPlayer").unbind("click").bind("click", function() {
				bugs.music.popWebPlayer();
				bugs.wiselog.area('M_header_02_20');
				return false;
			});
		}
	}
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
  var toggleNationLayer = function() {
    $("aside.selectNation").toggle(250, function(){});
  }

$(document).ready(function () {

  function changeTitle(){
    try{
              if('KR' != 'KR'){
        var newTitle = '벅스차트 > 곡 차트 > 대한민국 - 벅스';
        var curTitle = document.title;
        if(newTitle != curTitle){
          document.title = newTitle;
        } else {
          setTimeout(changeTitle, 500);
        }
      }
    } catch(e){}
  };

  changeTitle();

  $(document).click(function(ev){
    if( typeof($(ev.target).attr('class')) === 'undefined' ) return;
    if ($(ev.target).attr('class') != "selectedNationName"
        && ($(ev.target).attr('class').indexOf("flag") != 0  )
        && ($(ev.target).attr('class').indexOf("btnNation") == -1 ) ) {
          $("aside.selectNation").hide(250);
      }
    });
});
</script>

<script>
$(document).ready(function(){
			if(bugs.cookie.get('bside_coach_mark') != "N"){
			$('aside.coachConnect').show();
		}
});

function bsideCoachMarkClick(){
	var oDate = new Date();
	oDate.setDate(oDate.getDate() + 3650); //10 years...
	$('aside.coachConnect').hide();
	bugs.cookie.set('bside_coach_mark', 'N', oDate, "/");
}


</script>

				wiselogStr = "bugs.wiselog.area('S_sp_04_02');"

		}else{
			$('#contentsBanner3').addClass('lineBreak');
		}
		var currentWidth = 0;
		$(window).on('resize',function(){
			currentWidth = $(window).width();
			if(oldWidth < 1903 && 1903 <= currentWidth){
				$('#contentsBanner2').removeClass('lineBreak');
				$('#contentsBanner3').addClass('lineBreak');
			}else if(currentWidth < 1903 && 1903 <= oldWidth){
				$('#contentsBanner3').removeClass('lineBreak');
				$('#contentsBanner2').addClass('lineBreak');
			}
			oldWidth = currentWidth;
		});
		
		$('aside.contentsBanner').show();
	}
	
});

<script type="text/javascript" src="/js/jquery/jquery-dateFormat.min.js"></script>
<script>
$(window.document).ready(function() {
			setTimeout(function(){
				$.ajax({
					url : g_urlAjax + "/board/notice/ajax/commonfooternotice",
					type : "POST",
					dataType : "json",
					success : function(data){
						if(data != null){
							$("#commonFooterNotice a#commonFooterNoticeTitle").text(data.title);
							$("#commonFooterNotice a#commonFooterNoticeTitle").attr("href", g_urlMusic + "/board/notice?srl=" + data.srl + "&wl_ref=M_footer_01_01");
							$("#commonFooterNotice time").text(data.crt_dt);
							$("#commonFooterNotice time").attr("datetime", $.format.date(Date.parse(data.crt_dt,"yyyy.MM.dd"), "yyyy-MM-dd"));
						}
					}
				});
			}, 1300);

});
</script>
